    I-snowball-003a — ClaimGraph component + /runs/[runId]/graph route (GH#449)
    
    Per brief APPROVE'd by Codex iter 2/5 (`.codex/I-snowball-003a/codex_brief_verdict.txt`).
    
    Adds the F-snowball frontend:
    - GET /runs/{runId}/graph — Next.js client route fetching GraphPayload
      from `/api/runs/{run_id}/graph` (backend shipped via I-snowball-002).
    - <ClaimGraph> component wrapping react-cytoscapejs (SSR-unsafe;
      dynamic-import with ssr: false).
    - v1 server returns position: null so layout uses fcose
      (randomize: false, quality: 'proof', animate: false). When future
      I-snowball-002b adds server-side positions, every-positions check
      switches to preset layout automatically.
    - Idempotent cytoscape.use(fcose) registration (HMR-safe).
    - Tier-color styling: sentence/source/section/frame + bibliography_missing
      fallback nodes (dashed border). Edge-type styling: cites (thin blue) /
      contradicts (red, double-width) / section_member (grey dashed).
    - Loading + error states; data-testid hooks for I-snowball-006b Playwright.
    
    Packages added (all MIT runtime; @types/* devDeps):
    - cytoscape@3.30.4
    - react-cytoscapejs@2.0.0
    - cytoscape-fcose@2.2.0
    - @types/cytoscape, @types/react-cytoscapejs, @types/cytoscape-fcose
    
    Smoke: npm run typecheck + npm run lint pass cleanly (only pre-existing
    warnings unrelated to this PR remain).

 succeeded in 1812ms:
   1: """FastAPI route for F-snowball claim-graph endpoint.
   2: 
   3: `GET /api/runs/{run_id}/graph` returns a cytoscape-format `GraphPayload`
   4: built from the V30 AuditIR for one run. Server returns elements + a
   5: canonical content hash; the client computes layout positions in a Web
   6: Worker (DECISION.md Option B; positions are not populated server-side).
   7: 
   8: Per I-snowball-002 brief APPROVE'd by Codex iter 5 (2026-05-12).
   9: """
  10: 
  11: from __future__ import annotations
  12: 
  13: import hashlib
  14: import json
  15: import re
  16: from typing import Literal
  17: 
  18: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
  19: 
  20: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  21: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  22: 
  23: if TYPE_CHECKING:
  24:     from polaris_graph.audit_ir.loader import AuditIR
  25: 
  26: router = APIRouter(tags=["graph"])
  27: 
  28: # Lazy imports for audit_ir.{registry,loader} live inside `get_run_graph`
  29: # (Codex diff iter 1 P1): module-level imports trigger src/__init__.py →
  30: # .env load → optional real-backend wiring, which makes app startup +
  31: # this module's import non-hermetic. Keep graph_route import cheap.
  32: 
  33: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  34: # Type literals
  35: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  36: 
  37: NodeType = Literal["sentence", "source", "section", "frame"]
  38: EdgeType = Literal["cites", "contradicts", "section_member"]
  39: Tier = Literal["T1", "T2", "T3", "T4", "T5", "T6", "T7"]
  40: FrameStatus = Literal["pass", "partial", "fail"]
  41: 
  42: _VALID_TIERS = {"T1", "T2", "T3", "T4", "T5", "T6", "T7"}
  43: 
  44: 
  45: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  46: # Pydantic models
  47: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  48: 
  49: class NodeData(BaseModel):
  50:     id: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=300)
  51:     type: NodeType
  52:     label: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=500)
  53:     tier: Tier | None = None
  54:     sentence_text: str | None = None
  55:     source_url: str | None = None
  56:     section_title: str | None = None
  57:     frame_status: FrameStatus | None = None
  58:     classes: str | None = None
  59: 
  60: 
  61: class Position(BaseModel):
  62:     x: float
  63:     y: float
  64: 
  65: 
  66: class ClaimNode(BaseModel):
  67:     data: NodeData
  68:     position: Position | None = None  # Option B: None server-side; client populates
  69: 
  70: 
  71: class EdgeData(BaseModel):
  72:     id: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=400)
  73:     source: str
  74:     target: str
  75:     edge_type: EdgeType
  76: 
  77: 
  78: class ClaimEdge(BaseModel):
  79:     data: EdgeData
  80: 
  81: 
  82: class GraphElements(BaseModel):
  83:     nodes: list[ClaimNode]
  84:     edges: list[ClaimEdge]
  85: 
  86: 
  87: class GraphDiagnostics(BaseModel):
  88:     bibliography_count: int
  89:     fallback_source_count: int  # unique evidence_ids referenced but absent from bibliography
  90:     missing_reference_occurrence_count: int  # total references (with duplicates)
  91:     referenced_unknown_evidence_ids: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
  92: 
  93: 
  94: class GraphPayload(BaseModel):
  95:     elements: GraphElements
  96:     run_id: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
  97:     elements_hash: str = Field(min_length=64, max_length=64)
  98:     diagnostics: GraphDiagnostics
  99:     schema_version: Literal["1.0"] = "1.0"
 100: 
 101: 
 102: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 103: # Helpers
 104: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 105: 
 106: def _slug(text: str) -> str:
 107:     return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9]+", "_", text.lower()).strip("_")[:80] or "section"
 108: 
 109: 
 110: def _normalize_frame_status(raw: str) -> FrameStatus | None:
 111:     if raw == "pass":
 112:         return "pass"
 113:     if raw == "partial":
 114:         return "partial"
 115:     if raw.startswith("fail"):
 116:         return "fail"
 117:     return None
 118: 
 119: 
 120: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 121: # Builder (pure function — easy to test)
 122: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 123: 
 124: def build_graph_payload(ir: "AuditIR") -> GraphPayload:
 125:     """Transform AuditIR into cytoscape-format GraphPayload (deterministic)."""
 126:     # 1. Bibliography source nodes
 127:     bib_ids: set[str] = set()
 128:     nodes: list[ClaimNode] = []
 129:     for entry in ir.bibliography:
 130:         bib_ids.add(entry.evidence_id)
 131:         tier = entry.tier if entry.tier in _VALID_TIERS else None
 132:         label = (entry.statement or entry.evidence_id)[:200]
 133:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 134:             id=f"src:{entry.evidence_id}", type="source", label=label,
 135:             tier=tier, source_url=entry.url or None,
 136:         )))
 137: 
 138:     # 2. Collect all referenced evidence_ids from sentence tokens + contradictions
 139:     referenced_occurrences: list[str] = []
 140:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 141:         for sent in section.sentences:
 142:             if sent.is_verified:
 143:                 for tok in sent.tokens:
 144:                     referenced_occurrences.append(tok.evidence_id)
 145:     for cluster in ir.contradictions:
 146:         for claim in cluster.claims:
 147:             referenced_occurrences.append(claim.evidence_id)
 148:     referenced_unique = set(referenced_occurrences)
 149: 
 150:     # 3. Fallback source nodes for referenced-but-missing-from-bibliography
 151:     missing_unique = sorted(referenced_unique - bib_ids)
 152:     for eid in missing_unique:
 153:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 154:             id=f"src:{eid}", type="source", label=eid, classes="bibliography_missing",
 155:         )))
 156:     valid_source_ids = bib_ids | set(missing_unique)
 157: 
 158:     # 4. Section nodes
 159:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 160:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 161:             id=f"section:{_slug(section.title)}", type="section",
 162:             label=section.title, section_title=section.title,
 163:         )))
 164: 
 165:     # 5. Frame nodes (FrameCoverageReport.entries per AuditIR schema)
 166:     for entry in ir.frame_coverage.entries:
 167:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 168:             id=f"frame:{entry.entity_id}", type="frame", label=entry.entity_id,
 169:             frame_status=_normalize_frame_status(entry.status),
 170:         )))
 171: 
 172:     # 6. Sentence nodes + section_member + cites edges
 173:     edges: list[ClaimEdge] = []
 174:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 175:         sec_id = f"section:{_slug(section.title)}"
 176:         for sent in section.sentences:
 177:             if not sent.is_verified:
 178:                 continue
 179:             sent_id = f"sent:{sent.claim_id}"
 180:             nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 181:                 id=sent_id, type="sentence",
 182:                 label=sent.text[:100], sentence_text=sent.text,
 183:             )))
 184:             edges.append(ClaimEdge(data=EdgeData(
 185:                 id=f"membersec:{sent.claim_id}:{_slug(section.title)}",
 186:                 source=sent_id, target=sec_id, edge_type="section_member",
 187:             )))
 188:             for ord_, tok in enumerate(sent.tokens):
 189:                 if tok.evidence_id not in valid_source_ids:
 190:                     continue  # defensive — should not happen given fallback creation
 191:                 edges.append(ClaimEdge(data=EdgeData(
 192:                     id=f"cite:{sent.claim_id}:{ord_}:{tok.evidence_id}",
 193:                     source=sent_id, target=f"src:{tok.evidence_id}", edge_type="cites",
 194:                 )))
 195: 
 196:     # 7. Contradicts edges (pairwise within each cluster; skip self-contradictions)
 197:     for cluster in ir.contradictions:
 198:         evidence_ids = sorted({c.evidence_id for c in cluster.claims if c.evidence_id in valid_source_ids})
 199:         for i, a in enumerate(evidence_ids):
 200:             for b in evidence_ids[i + 1:]:
 201:                 edges.append(ClaimEdge(data=EdgeData(
 202:                     id=f"contra:{cluster.cluster_id}:{a}:{b}",
 203:                     source=f"src:{a}", target=f"src:{b}", edge_type="contradicts",
 204:                 )))
 205: 
 206:     # 8. Canonical content hash (position-stripped, sorted by id)
 207:     elements_dict = GraphElements(nodes=nodes, edges=edges).model_dump(mode="json")
 208:     elements_dict["nodes"].sort(key=lambda n: n["data"]["id"])
 209:     elements_dict["edges"].sort(key=lambda e: e["data"]["id"])
 210:     for n in elements_dict["nodes"]:
 211:         n.pop("position", None)
 212:     canonical = json.dumps(elements_dict, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":"))
 213:     elements_hash = hashlib.sha256(canonical.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
 214: 
 215:     return GraphPayload(
 216:         elements=GraphElements(nodes=nodes, edges=edges),
 217:         run_id=ir.run_id,
 218:         elements_hash=elements_hash,
 219:         diagnostics=GraphDiagnostics(
 220:             bibliography_count=len(bib_ids),
 221:             fallback_source_count=len(missing_unique),
 222:             missing_reference_occurrence_count=sum(
 223:                 1 for eid in referenced_occurrences if eid not in bib_ids
 224:             ),
 225:             referenced_unknown_evidence_ids=missing_unique,
 226:         ),
 227:     )
 228: 
 229: 
 230: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 231: # Route
 232: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 233: 
 234: @router.get("/runs/{run_id}/graph", response_model=GraphPayload)
 235: def get_run_graph(run_id: str) -> GraphPayload:
 236:     """Return cytoscape-format graph payload for a completed run."""
 237:     # Lazy import (Codex diff iter 1 P1): avoid loading audit_ir + .env at
 238:     # module load / app startup time.
 239:     from polaris_graph.audit_ir.loader import load_audit_ir
 240:     from polaris_graph.audit_ir.registry import find_run_by_id
 241: 
 242:     summary = find_run_by_id(run_id)
 243:     if summary is None:
 244:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="run not found")
 245:     try:
 246:         ir = load_audit_ir(summary.artifact_dir)
 247:     except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover
 248:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail=f"audit IR load failed: {exc}")
 249:     return build_graph_payload(ir)

   1: import { get as atKey } from './json';
   2: import { shallowObjDiff } from './diff';
   3: 
   4: const isDiffAtKey = (json1, json2, diff, key) =>
   5:   diff(atKey(json1, key), atKey(json2, key));
   6: 
   7: export const patch = (cy, json1, json2, diff, toJson, get, forEach) => {
   8:   cy.batch(() => {
   9:     // The shallow object diff() must defer to patchElements() as it must compare the
  10:     // elements as an unordered set.  A custom diff(), with Immutable for example,
  11:     // could just use an equality check (===).
  12:     if (
  13:       diff === shallowObjDiff ||
  14:       isDiffAtKey(json1, json2, diff, 'elements')
  15:     ) {
  16:       patchElements(
  17:         cy,
  18:         atKey(json1, 'elements'),
  19:         atKey(json2, 'elements'),
  20:         toJson,
  21:         get,
  22:         forEach,
  23:         diff
  24:       );
  25:     }
  26: 
  27:     if (isDiffAtKey(json1, json2, diff, 'stylesheet')) {
  28:       patchStyle(
  29:         cy,
  30:         atKey(json1, 'stylesheet'),
  31:         atKey(json2, 'stylesheet'),
  32:         toJson
  33:       );
  34:     }
  35: 
  36:     [
  37:       // simple keys that can be patched directly (key same as fn name)
  38:       'zoom',
  39:       'minZoom',
  40:       'maxZoom',
  41:       'zoomingEnabled',
  42:       'userZoomingEnabled',
  43:       'pan',
  44:       'panningEnabled',
  45:       'userPanningEnabled',
  46:       'boxSelectionEnabled',
  47:       'autoungrabify',
  48:       'autolock',
  49:       'autounselectify',
  50:     ].forEach((key) => {
  51:       if (isDiffAtKey(json1, json2, diff, key)) {
  52:         patchJson(cy, key, atKey(json1, key), atKey(json2, key), toJson);
  53:       }
  54:     });
  55:   });
  56: 
  57:   if (isDiffAtKey(json1, json2, diff, 'layout')) {
  58:     patchLayout(cy, atKey(json1, 'layout'), atKey(json2, 'layout'), toJson);
  59:   }
  60: };
  61: 
  62: const patchJson = (cy, key, val1, val2, toJson) => {
  63:   cy[key](toJson(val2));
  64: };
  65: 
  66: const patchLayout = (cy, layout1, layout2, toJson) => {
  67:   const layoutOpts = toJson(layout2);
  68: 
  69:   if (layoutOpts != null) {
  70:     cy.layout(layoutOpts).run();
  71:   }
  72: };

  74: const patchStyle = (cy, style1, style2, toJson) => {

  77:   if (style == null) {
  78:     return;
  79:   }
  80: 
  81:   style.fromJson(toJson(style2)).update();
  82: };

  84: const patchElements = (cy, eles1, eles2, toJson, get, forEach, diff) => {

  86:   const toRm = cy.collection();
  87:   const toPatch = [];

  89:   const eles2Map = {};

  91:   const eles2HasId = (id) => eles2Map[id] != null;
  92:   const getEle1 = (id) => eles1Map[id];
  93:   const getId = (ele) => get(get(ele, 'data'), 'id');
  94: 
  95:   forEach(eles2, (ele2) => {
  96:     const id = getId(ele2);
  97: 
  98:     eles2Map[id] = ele2;
  99:   });

  10:  */
  11: export default class CytoscapeComponent extends React.Component {
  12:   static get propTypes() {
  13:     return types;
  14:   }
  15: 
  16:   static get defaultProps() {
  17:     return defaults;
  18:   }
  19: 
  20:   static normalizeElements(elements) {
  21:     const isArray = elements.length != null;
  22: 
  23:     if (isArray) {
  24:       return elements;
  25:     } else {
  26:       let { nodes, edges } = elements;
  27: 
  28:       if (nodes == null) {
  29:         nodes = [];
  30:       }
  31: 
  32:       if (edges == null) {
  33:         edges = [];
  34:       }
  35: 
  36:       return nodes.concat(edges);
  37:     }
  38:   }
  39: 
  40:   constructor(props) {
  41:     super(props);

+"use client";
+
+import Link from "next/link";
+import { use, useEffect, useState } from "react";
+
+import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
+import { getRunGraph, type GraphPayload } from "@/lib/api";
+
+import { ClaimGraph } from "./components/claim_graph";
+
+interface GraphPageProps {
+  params: Promise<{ runId: string }>;
+}
+
+export default function GraphPage({ params }: GraphPageProps) {
+  const { runId } = use(params);
+  const [payload, setPayload] = useState<GraphPayload | null>(null);
+  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    let cancelled = false;
+    getRunGraph(runId)
+      .then((p) => {
+        if (!cancelled) setPayload(p);
+      })
+      .catch((e: Error) => {
+        if (!cancelled) setError(e.message);
+      });
+    return () => {
+      cancelled = true;
+    };
+  }, [runId]);
+
+  return (
+    <div className="flex min-h-screen flex-col">
+      <header className="border-border bg-background border-b">
+        <div className="mx-auto flex w-full max-w-6xl items-center justify-between px-6 py-4">
+          <div className="flex flex-col">
+            <span className="text-muted-foreground text-xs font-medium tracking-widest uppercase">
+              POLARIS — F-snowball
+            </span>
+            <span className="text-foreground text-base font-semibold">
+              Claim graph: {runId}
+            </span>
+          </div>
+          <Button
+            variant="outline"
+            nativeButton={false}
+            render={<Link href={`/inspector/${runId}`} />}
+          >
+            Back to Inspector
+          </Button>
+        </div>
+      </header>
+
+      <main
+        data-testid="graph-page"
+        className="mx-auto flex w-full max-w-6xl flex-1 flex-col gap-4 px-6 py-6"
+      >
+        {error && (
+          <div
+            role="alert"
+            className="border-destructive text-destructive rounded-md border p-4"
+          >
+            Failed to load graph: {error}
+          </div>
+        )}
+
+        {!payload && !error && (
+          <div
+            role="status"
+            className="text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2"
+          >
+            <span
+              aria-hidden
+              className="inline-block h-3 w-3 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-current border-t-transparent"
+            />
+            Loading graph for run {runId}…
+          </div>
+        )}
+
+        {payload && <ClaimGraph payload={payload} />}
+      </main>
+    </div>
+  );
+}

+    },
+  },
+  {
+    selector: "node.bibliography_missing",
+    style: {
+      "background-color": "#9ca3af",
+      "border-style": "dashed",
+      "border-width": 1,
+      "border-color": "#6b7280",
+    },
+  },
+  {
+    selector: "edge[edge_type='cites']",
+    style: {
+      "line-color": "#60a5fa",
+      width: 1,
+      "curve-style": "bezier",
+    },
+  },
+  {
+    selector: "edge[edge_type='contradicts']",
+    style: {
+      "line-color": "#ef4444",
+      width: 2,
+      "curve-style": "bezier",
+      "line-style": "solid",
+    },
+  },
+  {
+    selector: "edge[edge_type='section_member']",
+    style: {
+      "line-color": "#d4d4d4",
+      "line-style": "dashed",
+      width: 1,
+      opacity: 0.5,
+    },
+  },
+];
+
+const LAYOUT_FCOSE = {
+  name: "fcose",
+  randomize: false,
+  quality: "proof",
+  animate: false,
+  nodeSeparation: 75,
+  idealEdgeLength: 50,
+} as unknown as cytoscape.LayoutOptions;
+
+const LAYOUT_PRESET: cytoscape.LayoutOptions = { name: "preset" };
+
+export function ClaimGraph({ payload }: ClaimGraphProps) {
+  const { elements, layout } = useMemo(() => {
+    const hasPositions =
+      payload.elements.nodes.length > 0 &&
+      payload.elements.nodes.every((n) => n.position != null);
+
+    const cyNodes = payload.elements.nodes.map((n) => ({
+      data: n.data,
+      position: n.position ?? undefined,
+      classes: n.data.classes ?? undefined,
+    }));
+    const cyEdges = payload.elements.edges.map((e) => ({ data: e.data }));
+
+    return {
+      elements: [...cyNodes, ...cyEdges],
+      layout: hasPositions ? LAYOUT_PRESET : LAYOUT_FCOSE,
+    };
+  }, [payload]);
+
+  return (
+    <section
+      aria-label="Claim graph"
+      data-testid="claim-graph"
+      className="border-border flex w-full flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-md border"
+    >
+      <div className="h-[600px] w-full">
+        <CytoscapeComponent
+          elements={elements}
+          style={{ width: "100%", height: "100%" }}
+          layout={layout}
+          stylesheet={STYLESHEET}
+        />
+      </div>
+      <p className="text-muted-foreground border-border border-t p-2 text-xs">
+        {payload.elements.nodes.length} nodes · {payload.elements.edges.length}{" "}
+        edges · hash {payload.elements_hash.slice(0, 12)}…
+      </p>
+    </section>
+  );
+}

+// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+// F-snowball graph (I-snowball-002 backend + I-snowball-003a frontend).
+// Cytoscape-format graph payload mirroring src/polaris_graph/api/graph_route.py.
+// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+
+export type GraphNodeType = "sentence" | "source" | "section" | "frame";
+export type GraphEdgeType = "cites" | "contradicts" | "section_member";
+export type GraphTier = "T1" | "T2" | "T3" | "T4" | "T5" | "T6" | "T7";
+export type GraphFrameStatus = "pass" | "partial" | "fail";
+
+export interface GraphNodeData {
+  id: string;
+  type: GraphNodeType;
+  label: string;
+  tier?: GraphTier;
+  sentence_text?: string;
+  source_url?: string;
+  section_title?: string;
+  frame_status?: GraphFrameStatus;
+  classes?: string;
+}
+
+export interface GraphPosition {
+  x: number;
+  y: number;
+}
+
+export interface GraphNode {
+  data: GraphNodeData;
+  position?: GraphPosition | null;
+}
+
+export interface GraphEdgeData {
+  id: string;
+  source: string;
+  target: string;
+  edge_type: GraphEdgeType;
+}
+
+export interface GraphEdge {
+  data: GraphEdgeData;
+}
+
+export interface GraphDiagnostics {
+  bibliography_count: number;
+  fallback_source_count: number;
+  missing_reference_occurrence_count: number;
+  referenced_unknown_evidence_ids: string[];
+}
+
+export interface GraphPayload {
+  elements: { nodes: GraphNode[]; edges: GraphEdge[] };
+  run_id: string;
+  elements_hash: string;
+  diagnostics: GraphDiagnostics;
+  schema_version: "1.0";
+}
+
+export async function getRunGraph(runId: string): Promise<GraphPayload> {
+  const res = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/runs/${runId}/graph`);
+  if (!res.ok) {
+    const body = await res.text();
+    const err = new Error(
+      `getRunGraph(${runId}) HTTP ${res.status}: ${body}`,
+    ) as ApiError;
+    err.status = res.status;
+    throw err;
+  }
+  return res.json() as Promise<GraphPayload>;
+}
